5/11/25, 19:16 - Luis Premiumguest: I was uploading a pending bulk change to the terms and conditions listed on the ticket.

We have a tool that allows us to make this change to a large volume of ticket types at once. What happened was that I did it using Google Sheets, and in the price section, the format I had in that Excel spreadsheet, for example, €1,000, was showing up with a period.

When I uploaded that file to the system for the change, because the period was present in the 1000, it was translating the value as €1.
5/11/25, 19:18 - Luis Premiumguest: Once we realized the error, we tried to react as quickly as possible, and that's why we changed the website link to prevent any erroneous sales.

Everything has now been reviewed, and there are no entries with values ​​affected by this.

We sincerely apologize; we're sorry!

2/4/26, 14:12 - +34 690 80 56 65: Initiate Checkout is typically an event that is tracked when a user starts the process of completing a purchase on an eCommerce site. This usually happens when a customer clicks on the checkout button or when the checkout page is loaded.

To help your product team understand what you're trying to achieve, here's an example of how these two events might work:

Add to Cart: This event is triggered when a user adds an item to their shopping cart. It helps you track the number of items being considered for purchase.

Initiate Checkout: This event would be triggered when the user proceeds from their cart to the checkout page. It's a critical moment in the purchase journey, as it indicates that the user is ready to complete the transaction, but hasn't yet submitted payment or finalised the order.

The typical base code for add to card for our pixel 203773703560465 would be

  if(!f._fbq)f._fbq=n;n.push=n;n.loaded=!0;n.version='2.0';
  n.queue=[];t=b.createElement(e);t.async=!0;
  t.src=v;s=b.getElementsByTagName(e)[0];s.parentNode.insertBefore(t,s)}(window, document,'script',
  'https://connect.facebook.net/en_US/fbevents.js');

  });
</script>
